              <a href="https://docs.taurushq.com/prime/reference/balanceservice_getbalances" class="text-pink-500 hover:text-pink-600 inline-flex items-center gap-1">
                Rest-API access <span aria-hidden="true">↗</span>
              </a><br>
              <a href="https://docs.taurushq.com/prime/docs/fix-introduction" class="text-pink-500 hover:text-pink-600 inline-flex items-center gap-1">
                FIX access <span aria-hidden="true">↗</span>
              </a>
            </div>
          </article>

          <!-- Taurus User Guides -->
          <article class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm p-7 flex flex-col justify-between">
            <div>
              <div class="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-10 h-10 rounded-xl text-white mb-4">
                <span class="text-lg font-semibold"><img src="https://images.taurusgroup.ch/protect/taurus-doc.png" class="product-icon"></span>
              </div>
              <h3 class="text-sm font-semibold mb-2">
                Taurus User Guides
              </h3>
              <p class="text-xs leading-relaxed text-gray-600 mb-4">
                Comprehensive documentation and guides to help you integrate and build with Taurus products. Everything you need to succeed.
              </p>
            </div>
            <p class="text-[11px] text-gray-400 font-medium">
              Restricted access
            </p>
          </article>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- Why Taurus Developer Platform -->
    <section class="bg-gray-50 py-16 lg:py-20">
      <div class="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 text-center mb-12">
        <h2 class="text-3xl md:text-4xl font-extrabold tracking-tight mb-3">
          Why Taurus Developer Platform?
        </h2>
      </div>

      <div class="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-4 grid gap-8 md:grid-cols-3">
        <!-- Security at the core -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm p-8 text-left">
          <h3 class="text-base font-semibold mb-3 text-pink-500">Security at the core</h3>
          <p class="text-sm leading-relaxed text-gray-600">
            Built with institutional-grade security from the ground up. Multi-layered protection,
            compliance-ready infrastructure, and battle-tested protocols ensure your assets and data
            remain secure.
          </p>
        </div>

        <!-- Composable Architecture -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm p-8 text-left">
          <h3 class="text-base font-semibold mb-3 text-pink-500">Composable Architecture</h3>
          <p class="text-sm leading-relaxed text-gray-600">
            Our modular platform can support a very broad range of use cases, from cryptocurrencies to stablecoins and tokenized securities.
            Seamless integration between services lets you build exactly what you envision.
          </p>
        </div>

        <!-- Scale with Confidence -->
        <div class="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm p-8 text-left">
          <h3 class="text-base font-semibold mb-3 text-pink-500">Scale with Confidence</h3>
          <p class="text-sm leading-relaxed text-gray-600">
            Our platform is built to scale. API-first, handle millions of transactions with
            low latency and high availability backed by robust infrastructure.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

Requests are typically verified and approved (signed) by one or more approvers as defined in Governance rules. A single request can result in multiple blockchain transactions.","_id":"69724fceb29a6f04bf489471"},{"term":"Transaction","definition":"A transaction represents a blockchain transaction as observed on the blockchain network. Requests are typically verified and approved (signed) by one or more approvers as defined in Governance rules.
